Resolution of the Longjing Village Incident

Both China and Japan have indicated their commitment to resolving the Sino-Japanese military police conflict in Longjing Village, Jilin. As reported previously, the situation shifted rapidly after the Japanese police withdrew on the 6th of this month. It is now learned that the original Japanese demands included: (1) 20,000 Japanese yen in compensation for each of the three Japanese policemen killed; (2) A formal apology from Chinese officials at the Japanese Consulate General; (3) Punishment of those responsible for the incident; (4) A guarantee that similar incidents would not occur in the future. After several rounds of negotiations between Zhang Shuhan, Director of the Yanji Municipal Preparatory Office, and Mr. Okada, the Japanese Consul General stationed in Longjing, their opinions gradually converged. On the 9th, Mr. Zhang, accompanied by Secretary Feng, went to Longjing again to continue negotiations with Mr. Okada. After deliberation, it was agreed that the Chinese side would provide 10,000 Japanese yen as a condolence payment, expressing regret for the deaths of the Japanese policemen. The Japanese side withdrew its demand for punishment, and the army personnel involved would be given appropriate punishment by the Chinese side on the grounds of misunderstanding. Consul General Okada would telegraph his government, and Mr. Zhang would telegraph the Jilin Provincial Government to request instructions. The Provincial Government has already replied, instructing him to proceed accordingly. Mr. Okada has also received instructions and personally visited Yanji on the 11th for a final meeting with Director Zhang. By the 13th, both parties had expressed their commitment to the above-mentioned arrangements, and the case was completely resolved. Only a small portion of the procedures remain. Furthermore, after the Japanese police withdrew, the Japanese consul informed the Chinese side that the local security would still be the responsibility of the Chinese side, which is considered a statement regarding the Japanese withdrawal of police. (15th)

Extensive Police Inspection of White Russians in Harbin

Due to Protest from the Soviet Consul in Harbin. Harbin Communication: Mr. Melnikov, the Soviet Consul General in Harbin, lodged a protest with our Foreign Affairs Commissioner last week, stating that the Chinese authorities, according to the Borly Agreement, should not tolerate White Russians engaging in political activities and anti-Soviet movements in the Special Zone, or distributing leaflets that are detrimental to Soviet Russia. If the Chinese authorities do not crack down on these activities, it would be seen as deliberately inciting White Russians to take actions detrimental to Soviet Russia, and the Soviet Union will take appropriate measures to ensure the safety of important personnel in Harbin. At the same time, Znamensky, the Soviet Consul General in Liaoning, also protested to the local Jiaotong Department, listing the residences and activities of White Russian leaders. After receiving the protest letter forwarded by the Foreign Affairs Commissioner, the Northeast Political Affairs Committee telegraphed the Special Zone Administrator's Office, ordering a thorough inspection of the addresses provided to verify whether the allegations made by the Russian consul regarding the White Russians in Harbin were true. The Administrator's Office then instructed the Special Police Department to be responsible for the inspection. On the 14th of this month, the Investigation Bureau of the Special Police Department was ordered to handle this matter. The first inspection was conducted at No. 104 Dazhi Street, Qinjiagang. According to the Russian consul, the house was inhabited by former Russian generals (Baorge Lujiweisi Ji) and (Sichefu), who had formed an alliance of White Russian soldiers and secretly gathered loyal supporters as a powerful group to resist Soviet Russia. However, the Investigation Bureau found nothing during the inspection on that day. General Baorge Lujiweisi Ji had secretly arrived in Harbin from the Primorsky Krai last month and had recently gone to Shanghai. There was no political organization as claimed by the Russian consul. The residence of Sichefu at No. 7 Tongdao Street, Qinjiagang, was also inspected on the same day, but nothing was found. In the afternoon, inspections were also conducted at sixteen locations of the White Russian Youth Association and the Student Association, but no suspicious signs were found. On the 15th and 16th, inspections were continued in various places, but nothing was found. However, according to the list of suspicious individuals provided by the Russian consul: (1) Nazalov, of the National Corps of Russian Citizens Fighting Against the Third International, printed anti-Soviet documents at the Harbin Daily News Printing Company; (2) Sushkov, the leader of the former Russian Eagle Squad, lived at No. 13 Xiehe Street, Majiagou, and the important officials of the squad

Bao Bao, lived at No. 20 Xinmaimai Street, at the Printing Office; (3) Glizov, the president of the Russian Truth Brotherhood, lived at No. 19 Fengtian Hotel, Nangang, and the printing of anti-Soviet documents was undertaken by the Fengtai Printing Office in Daoli; (4) Bokrovsky, the president of the National Assembly League, printed anti-Soviet documents at the Facai Printing Office at the corner of Central Avenue; (5) Mu Deli Ning, the commander of the Votkinsk Army Izhevites National Corps, currently lived on Majie Street; (6) Kuoluo Kuoli Ni Kuofu, the president of the Harbin Russian Refugee Relief Association, was located at No. 16 Youzheng Street, Nangang; (7) Grachev, the leader of the Farmers' and Workers' Corps, lived at No. 322 JieJing Street, Majiagou; (8) Longwei Li Yefu, the commander of the Ussuri Cavalry Army, was in contact with the Yingzi Army; (9) Leader Semyonov's movement group lived at No. 16 Jiaotang Street, Majiagou. Jilin Chamber of Commerce Appeals to the Central Government to Revise the Chamber of Commerce Law

Listing Three Reasons for the Amendment. Shenyang Communication: The Jilin Provincial Chamber of Commerce recently sent a telegram to Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang, appealing to him to propose to the central government amendments to the implementing regulations of the Chamber of Commerce Law to safeguard commercial operations. The telegram reads as follows: (We have found that since the promulgation of the newly enacted Chamber of Commerce Law and its implementing regulations, the commercial sector across the country has collectively opposed them unanimously. Regarding the new law, the points that various General Chambers of Commerce and Chambers of Commerce find difficult to accept can be summarized as follows: (1) The new law stipulates that the number of executive committee members of the Chamber of Commerce is only fifteen, which is too small. The number of personnel should be increased. It is also found that in large commercial ports, there are many guilds and industries. The executive committee is the crystallization of the consensus of merchants, and the number of members must be slightly broader to avoid industries feeling left out during elections. The new law only stipulates fifteen executive committee members, which cannot represent the interests of the entire commercial sector, and the drawbacks will inevitably lead to difficulties in handling affairs and repeated failures. It is urgent to revise this in accordance with the organizational outline approved by the provincial chambers of commerce, setting the number of members of the General Chamber of Commerce at forty-nine and the number of members of the Chamber of Commerce at twenty-five. This is the first amendment that should be made. (2) The name of the General Chamber of Commerce should be preserved, and the format of official documents should remain unchanged. The establishment of the General Chamber of Commerce and the Chamber of Commerce is based on the complexity of commerce and the size of the commercial port. The establishment of the General Chamber of Commerce is in a province or a large port. Its geographic location is important, and its commerce is prosperous. Therefore, the word "General" is added to the name to show its importance. The power of jurisdiction belongs to the highest local administrative official, so that they can make convenient petitions and avoid delays and difficulties. This was carefully considered when the law was originally drafted and has been implemented for many years without any problems. The current Chamber of Commerce Law not only eliminates the name of the General Chamber of Commerce, but also stipulates that the procedures for official documents must be submitted to the local county and municipal governments for review and transfer, reducing the scope of the Chamber of Commerce and reducing the powers of the Chamber of Commerce, which is clearly inconsistent with democratic centralism. This is the second amendment that should be made. (3) The official seal of the General Chamber of Commerce and the Chamber of Commerce should remain in its original form and not be changed. Since the names of the General Chamber of Commerce and the Chamber of Commerce are different, the trust and respect should not be the same. Furthermore, it has been implemented for many years, and officials and merchants have been at peace. This is essentially a matter of form and has nothing to do with the overall situation. Why should it be changed? It is necessary to order that they all be changed to use the seal, which is nothing more than depriving the Chamber of Commerce of its power. This kind of proposition seems unreasonable. This is the third amendment that should be made. In summary, the Chamber of Commerce is a legal organization of merchants, originally established to seek commercial development and enhance the welfare of the commercial sector. In recent years, during the rise of the revolutionary army, raising funds and soliciting debts, the commercial sector across the country has spared no effort to support the revolution. It has made considerable achievements in the history of the revolution. Now, fortunately, the revolution has been completed. Although we dare not ask for rewards, the status and treatment of the General Chamber of Commerce and the Chamber of Commerce should not be maintained as before. Furthermore, we must be subject to various constraints and restrictions. The matter is unfair and painful to speak of. Although the chambers of commerce in various provinces and regions have repeatedly petitioned the central government, there have been no results. Now, fortunately, the overall situation has been settled. It is a time for the people of the whole country to work hard on construction. The Chamber of Commerce is a legal organization without an appropriate legal system. We have always admired your seat for protecting merchants and upholding justice. Therefore, we appeal to you with all our heart to approve the proposal to the central government to revise the Chamber of Commerce Law and its implementing regulations to safeguard commercial operations and comfort public opinion. We are awaiting orders with utmost urgency. (November 18th)

Disputes in the Shandong Hat-Making Industry

German Merchants Fail to Fulfill Contract, Labor Decides to Protest. Qingdao Communication: The Baohe Foreign Firm Juji Accounting House, a German merchant in Qingdao, established a model factory for women's hat weaving in Jiaoxian County this spring, recruiting more than 30 female students. After graduation, factories were established in Jiaoxian, Jimo, Pingdu, Gaomi, and other counties, with one general contractor for each factory. A contract was signed with the most important condition being that all raw materials would be supplied by the capital side, and after production, they would still be sold to foreigners. The teachers would also be dispatched by the capital side. Within two years, the contractors of the factories could not resell the goods produced by the factories to other merchants. Furthermore, all costs related to teaching fees, practice grass weaving materials, etc., and hat weaving wages would be provided by the accounting house. Within a few months of opening, the number of expanded factories reached more than 13 counties, with about hundreds of factories and more than 10,000 workers. These workers were purely women, and those with excellent skills could make two to three grass hats per month (this type of hat is made of flax fabric and is meticulously handmade), while those with ordinary skills could make one to two hats. The wages per hat were about four or five yuan, and each person could earn more than ten yuan per month. Unexpectedly, the foreign firm's accounting house has recently violated the contract. Initially, the teaching fees were changed to be borne by the contractors, and then the practice grass and all other costs were also changed to be borne by the contractors. At that time, the contractors of each factory had a large amount of money advanced for labor costs, and they could not afford to stop, so they had to endure the pain silently. Later, the accounting house refused to provide workers with materials and only accepted grass hats without paying wages, resulting in each factory having losses of up to five or six million yuan. At that time, more than 10,000 female workers were also unemployed. Recently, the accounting house has gathered the contractors of each factory to a meeting at the accounting house, ordering them to hand over all the materials issued before, whether completed or not, and to dismiss them all uniformly, otherwise, they would be severely punished. The contractors of each factory have united and protested against the Juji Accounting House's violation of regulations and destruction of labor, which is unbearable, and they have requested assistance from all walks of life. (November 18th)

Jiangsu Province Business Tax Collection Registration Fee Issue

Wuxi Chamber of Commerce Telegraphed the Central Government to Request Instructions for Clarification, and Asked to Suspend Collection Before Receiving a Reply. Wuxi Communication: Jiangsu Province is launching a business tax collection registration fee, and the provincial government has appointed Zhu Shengwu as the director of the Wuxi collection, implementing the collection. The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly received requests from various related industries and specially convened a meeting of representatives of various industries at 4 pm yesterday to discuss and resolve the issue. After deliberation, it was deemed that there were issues that should be resolved first, and the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce was telegraphed to take the lead in submitting a request to the central government for clarification, and before receiving a reply from the central government, the provincial government was requested to temporarily suspend the collection of business tax collection registration fees. After the meeting, the Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram on behalf of the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce that night, the original text is as follows: (The Fourth National Industry and Commerce Conference on November 5th, according to Article 8 of the Ministry of Finance's Outline of Methods for Collecting Business Tax in Various Provinces, stipulated that the collection of business tax must be carried out after the abolition of Likin is implemented. It was resolved that Jiangsu Province's plan to prepare for the collection of business tax registration fees does not comply with the Outline set by the Ministry. It is proposed that it is not necessary to formulate other transitional measures within the shortest period of time for the abolition of Likin, such as the Jiangsu Province's plan to prepare for the collection of business tax registration fees. Furthermore, the Sixth Item of Clause C of the plan to rejuvenate politics and establish the center of governance in the shortest period of time, which was resolved by the Fourth Plenary Session on November 17th, also stipulated that Likin and traffic surcharges similar to Likin will be abolished on January 1, 1931. The provinces must not request an extension for any reason. Furthermore, Clause 5 of the declaration resolved on November 18th also decided to abolish the Likin system on January 1, 1931, in order to reduce the burden on the people, eliminate the malpractices of decades, and promote the revitalization of industry and commerce. This is the sincerity of the central government and an important decision of this meeting. With the abolition of Likin having a fixed date, business tax is bound to be implemented, and there is no need to have another transition and collect registration fees. It is true that after the abolition of Likin, as stated in the original proposal resolved by the Industry and Commerce Conference, business tax can be conducted openly and fairly according to the provisions of the Outline, and it is not necessary to take advantage of the opportunity to add additional burdens to merchants and people in this short period of time. However, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance has submitted the Regulations on the Preparation for the Collection of Business Tax Registration Fees in Jiangsu Province and its Implementing Rules to the provincial government meeting for approval and promulgation, and ordered the counties to start operating as soon as possible. Upon investigation, Article 1, Section 2 of the Outline set by the Ministry stipulates that business licenses are renewed annually without charging a license fee. The Jiangsu Province's plan to prepare for the collection of business tax registration fees already contradicts the Outline set by the Ministry, and Article 2 of its regulations stipulates that those who have already obtained a registration certificate will be issued a magnetic tablet for a fee of 20 cents, and Article 10 stipulates that whether a business registration certificate is newly obtained or renewed, a fee of 20 cents will be charged for each certificate. In addition to the registration fee, there is also a magnetic tablet fee and a registration certificate fee, which further violates the new Outline. Not to mention that the Jiang Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed, based on Article 2, Section 2 of the Outline set by the Ministry, which stipulates that the types and conditions of business and the special circumstances in each province may be proposed separately, with variable methods and tax standards reported to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation, but the tax rate levied may not be higher than the provisions of this Outline. It was repeatedly stated that the Outline set by the Ministry should be used as the basis and six matters should be taken into consideration. It should be invited to public opinion. Upon investigation, Article 1 of the Outline set by the Ministry stipulates that business tax is local revenue, and all those who engage in commerce and open shops within the territory of each province, except for companies registered by the central government and those who have already had special taxes collected by the central government, must apply for a business license and pay business tax. Companies registered by the central government and those who have already had special taxes collected by the central government should be excluded from the scope of taxation. This is one point. Furthermore, Article 2 stipulates that the businesses subject to taxation include the sale of goods, manufacturing, printing, hotels, inns, entertainment venues, photography, dentistry, contracting, leasing of goods, transportation, money shops, pawnshops, and warehouses, which are listed clearly. Those that are not listed are naturally not subject to taxation. This is the second point. Furthermore, Article 4 stipulates that the following types are not subject to business tax: (1) those with capital less than 500 yuan, (2) those with annual income less than 1,000 yuan, (3) those without shop names, and (4) firewood industry. The above types, even if they are listed in Article 2, are not subject to business tax. This is the third point. Furthermore, Article 7 stipulates that after the implementation of business tax, all existing tooth sticker taxes, donation sticker taxes, slaughter taxes, etc., and other donations and taxes of the same nature as business tax in each province shall be separately merged or abolished. After the implementation of business tax, all existing tooth sticker taxes, donation sticker taxes, and slaughter taxes shall be merged or abolished. This is the fourth point. Furthermore, business tax is local revenue according to Article 1 of the Outline set by the Ministry, and there are currently four levels of provinces, counties, districts, towns, and townships. If it is over-emphasized at the provincial level, it will cause local disputes. How should it be divided or properly allocated? It seems that the Ministry should determine this in advance to avoid future disputes between local areas and the repeated burdens on merchants and people. This is the fifth point. Furthermore, Article 9 of the Outline set by the Ministry stipulates that the implementing rules for the collection of business tax shall be formulated by each province based on the provisions of this Outline and reported to the Ministry for record. The special circumstances in each province may propose separate variable methods and tax standards, which are all summarized within the scope of the implementing rules and must not formulate regulations that conflict with the Outline set by the Ministry. This is very clear. The current Jiangsu Province's Regulations on Business Tax Registration Fees not only fundamentally conflict with the Outline set by the Ministry, but also Article 2 separately collects magnetic license fees, Article 3 increases the registration fee for imported goods, Article 10 separately collects registration fees, and Article 11 imposes a penalty of two times the amount that should be supplemented for those who do not record their business or conceal short reports. These all do not comply with the Outline set by the Ministry. This is the sixth point. Furthermore, Article 3 of the Jiangsu Province's Regulations on Business Tax Registration Fees stipulates that businesses that mainly engage in imported goods will be singled out and have their capital amount increased by 5 per mille. This seems to be aimed at resisting foreign goods. However, upon careful examination of Article 2 of the Outline set by the Ministry, which lists the various businesses subject to taxation, there is no special provision for imported goods. This is not because it does not know the intention of resisting foreign goods, but because imported goods should be taxed by the customs according to the weight of the goods, and the business tax is based on the operation of commerce and opening of shops according to Article 1 of the Outline set by the Ministry.

Page 9

Without Non-Adding Further, While Most Inland Shops Agree That It Would Be Difficult To Distinguish Between Domestic And Foreign Goods; This Is The Seventh Point. It Is Now Confirmed That The Purpose of The Two Brigade's Struggle Was To Gain Control of The Unfrozen Port of The Area, The Shark River. The Two Factions Opened Fire And Fought For Two Nights. Shen Guanshou, The Leader of The North Faction, Was No Match For Pan Kaiwu And Others of The South Faction, And The Shark River Was Still Occupied By Them. Pan Has Continuously Persecuted Shen's Forces, Intending To Eliminate Shen. Shen Specially Proposed To Chen On The Day Before Yesterday That He Should Cooperate With Pan In Order To Maintain His Original Strength.

The Leak of Spring Light Caused A Storm. Xu, The Wife Of Chen, A Resident of Lifazhennan, Had A Cousin Who Was Only Fourteen Years Old And Possessed Some Beauty. Many People Wanted To Approach Her, But It Was Difficult To Achieve Their Goals Because Her Older Sister Supervised Her Strictly. However, Chen Xu Had An Unbreakable Bond With Zhao In The Town. Zhao Admired Her Cousin's Appearance And Often Teased Her, So He Had Secretly Passed Chencang This Spring And Seemed To Be Her Wife And Concubine. Now The Girl Is Two Months Pregnant And The Spring Light Has Been Leaked, Which Was Known To The Girl's Mother's Family. They Argued With Chen Xu, And Chen Xu Also Knew That She Had Misled Herself And Others, So She Demanded 200 Yuan From Zhao To Settle The Matter. Yesterday (The 14th), Zhao's Wife Heard About The Matter And Was Uncontrollably Angry. She Committed Suicide By Jumping Into The River, But Fortunately She Was Rescued By Spectators And Was Able To Rejoice In Her Rebirth. It Is Unknown How This Will Be Resolved.

Huzhou

Shaxi Tian Stores Robbed: At Shaxi Tian, about ten miles outside the north gate of this city, there are more than twenty stores, large and small. Unexpectedly, at about 2 a.m. yesterday, a dozen or so robbers, their faces covered with cloth, each holding guns, iron bars, and electric torches, and speaking in mixed dialects, suddenly arrived at the village. They robbed stores in different directions. The robbed businesses included Che Tongxing, Futai, and Tongchang grain and general merchandise stores, suffering a total loss of over four hundred yuan.

Large Numbers of Refugees Disturb Beishi Village: In Yuanjia Hui in Huzhou, a large number of refugees, three to four hundred, from Jianshi, Shuanglin, and other places arrived. The Public Security Bureau's Patrol Chief Shen and Sergeant Li temporarily detained them in Beishi Village. Unexpectedly, that place is an isolated hillock surrounded by water with no land route. The refugees then scattered to the villagers' homes, taking the name of collecting firewood and drinking tea, and arbitrarily seizing clothing and money. Dozens of families in the village were spared no losses, with the wealthiest Wang Xinfu family suffering the greatest loss. Afterwards, the village committee reported to the Yuanjia Hui water police and telegraphed the county government in this city for instructions. Ultimately, because the number of refugees was too large, there was no way to investigate. Only a dozen or so boats were hired to escort them to the Qingshan area and released them on the highway.

Xiaoshan

Regulations for Levying Baojia Special Tax: The Xiaoshan County Government recently received orders from the provincial government to implement Baojia (local self-defense system) and stipulated the collection of a Baojia special tax, using the amount of farmland as the standard for collection. It is divided into four grades: (1) those with 200 mu or more are Grade A, collecting a special tax of two yuan; (2) those with 100 mu or more are Grade B, collecting one yuan; (3) those with 50 mu or more are Grade C, collecting three jiao; (4) those with less than 50 mu are Grade D, collecting one jiao.

Chamber of Commerce Reorganization Established: The Xiaoshan County Chamber of Commerce has been reorganized into the Commerce Integration Association. The members took office successively starting on the 17th. Among the members, including Wang Xiufu, Chen Xiangfan, Huang Keqin, Xu Shuiying, Shen Qingfu, Chen Nianzu, and Zhang Wangyun, Chen Nianzu, Wang Xiufu, and Yu Keqin were elected as standing committee members, with Shen Qinfu as the director of the registration section and Xu Shuiying as the director of the investigation section. Chen Xiangfan is the secretary. Each section has added a secretary and an assistant to handle matters in phases. The official opening is scheduled for the 24th of this month.

Ningbo

Robbery Outside the South Gate: In Zhu Songlin and Zhu Defu's homes outside the south gate of the city, six bandits suddenly arrived at one o'clock yesterday morning, each holding sharp knives and breaking in. It is estimated that they stole silver dollars, clothes, and other items, each suffering a loss of more than one hundred yuan. After the bandits plundered, they fled to the southwest tombs.

Eighty-Four Extortion Letters: Three people were kidnapped from Shimen Village, Yanyuan District, Fenghua, last month. The ransom for one person was 10,000 yuan, and the other two were 2,000 yuan each. Efforts are currently being made to redeem them. Unexpectedly, yesterday, the village suddenly received a large number of extortion letters from bandits, as many as eighty-four. The asking prices were divided into four grades: Grade A 3,000 yuan, Grade B 2,000 yuan, Grade C 1,000 yuan, and Grade D 500 yuan. The villagers were deeply panicked after receiving the letters.

Long-Distance Telephone to Set Up Agencies: The Zhejiang Long-Distance Telephone Bureau, with its branch in Kaimingfang, Yong City, seeing the growing business, felt the need to establish more agencies. Therefore, the bureau specially sent Mr. Li to Yong City a few days ago to investigate the possibility of setting up three agencies in the county area and four agencies in the urban area. It is reported that four locations have been preliminarily designated in the urban area: Jiangbei, Jiangdong, Jiangxia, and Ximen.

Re-Pricing of Municipal Public Land for Public Auction: The Yong City Construction Committee held its sixth regular meeting yesterday afternoon and resolved to re-evaluate and schedule the auction of thirteen plots of municipal public land. The location and price of the public land are as follows: The remaining land on Dasha Ni Street is reduced to 25,000 yuan per mu; the Yong'an Bridge filled river foundation is reduced to 6,000 yuan per mu; the Malan River public land is reduced to 10,000 yuan per mu; the Xiangyang River foundation is reduced to 6,000 yuan per mu; one plot of land at Lingqiao Gate is set at 80,000 yuan per mu; the land next to the Nanyang Hotel under Chuanjia Bridge is 25,000 yuan per mu; another plot of land under Chuanjia Bridge is 15,000 yuan per mu; the Zhikou Alley land at Dongmenkou is 100,000 yuan per mu; the land behind Qiaomenyuan is 12,000 yuan per mu; the land at Xiadaotou is 60,000 yuan per mu; and the land under Qinglong Bridge on Xiaosha Ni Street is 6,000 yuan per mu. If the above-mentioned land for sale has adjacent owners, they should be given priority to purchase.

Special Article

Preface to the Recompiled Catalog of the Tianyige Collection

Several months ago, my friend Yang Ziyi took office as the mayor of Ningbo. I repeatedly wrote to him, urging him to reorganize the books in the Tianyige collection and compile a new catalog, holding the Fan clan jointly responsible for its preservation. Ziyi followed my advice. The account given by his secretary, Mr. Yang, is quite detailed. It is clear that the essence of the Tianyige collection has been almost completely lost, and even a single paper rubbing of bronzes and stone inscriptions remains. It is truly lamentable. The treasures of the world that have disappeared from the Tianyige collection are certainly not limited to the Huashan and Liu Xiong steles. The Tianyige of Xia'an was the place where Fan Shilang Yaoqing of the Ming dynasty stored his books. Siming's collection of books was led by Feng of Chengxi. Feng was a descendant of the Song dynasty's Qingmin Duke. His family had the Ten Thousand Volumes Tower, which contained many famous Song and Yuan dynasty xylographs. After several generations, about seventeen or eight out of ten were lost due to burning, destruction, borrowing, and theft. When they were gathered and returned to the Tianyige, they were specifically left behind by his son. Shilang obtained them and borrowed and copied what Yan Zhou had collected to supplement them. Moreover, he always personally wrote down the dates he obtained them. Therefore, the printed editions of the books are all from before the Tianqi era, and the manuscript copies are also not items that circulated in the market. As for those that included early Qing dynasty versions, they were added by his descendants and not touched by Shilang's hand. Therefore, although there were several book collections at the time, the Fan family was particularly known for its ancient books. Shilang divided his property and estimated the value of the books at ten thousand taels of silver, all to be inherited by one son. It cannot be said that his handling of the books was not good. After another generation, the locks and keys were very strict. Family rules stipulated that descendants could not go upstairs unless all branches of the family agreed, and they were not allowed to take books off the steps or privately lead relatives and friends to tour the blessed land. The strictness of the gate was equal to that of the imperial archives. Therefore, for decades between the Ming and Qing dynasties, spiderwebs and dust sealed off the floor, and it was nearly devoid of human traces, only arousing scholars' envy and speculative efforts. During the Qianlong era, an imperial edict was issued to seek out surviving books throughout the empire for the Siku Quanshu (Complete Library of the Four Treasuries). His descendant, Maozhu, selected 622 books to present to the emperor, who rewarded him with the Complete Illustrations and Commentary on the Book of History and the Illustrated Account of Military Achievements in the Pacification of the Hui Regions. He also personally inscribed the Wei Liaoweng's Zhouyi Yaoyi and Ma Zong's Yibei, which were among the books he presented, to show his favor and returned the remaining books he presented. He ordered weaving officials to personally visit his home to examine the methods of book collection, deeming it a model for the Tianlu Library. However, the catalog of the books remained unknown to outsiders. Initially, Mr. Huang Lizhou, due to his great prestige and friendship, was allowed to visit the pavilion as an exception and selected the most ancient and obscure books to copy into a catalog, which was circulated among people in Kunshan Jie Lu, so people began to know that there was a catalog of books in Tianyige, while the catalog of inscriptions was seen in Mr. Qian Xinbo's Yin Zhi. During the Jiaqing era, when Ruan Wenda governed Zhejiang, he began to engrave the catalog and write a preface to it. Since then, the Tianyige book catalog began to be published to the world. The catalog contained 4,094 books, 53,799 volumes. The catalog of inscriptions contained 764 kinds, which was also a grand sight. Since then, it suffered misfortune. During the Taiping Rebellion, Ningbo was a battlefield. Tian Wu Zhui Ku Lunyu Daixin was the first calamity. The founding of the Republic of China also suffered from its effects. Those who carried them away in bundles often fell into the hands of the Jiangbei Christian Church. After negotiation, they were allowed to be redeemed, but they were no longer perfect. This was the second calamity. The pavilion was sealed off, and those in charge regarded it as supremely sacred. However, the wall climbers took advantage of its uninhabited state. Once they managed to climb over the wall and break the window, they could calmly advance and retreat. This was the third calamity. Moreover, since people loved ancient artifacts, cases of digging up homes became increasingly common, and the techniques of stealing books became increasingly clever. Hidden paths were shifted and transformed invisibly. Looking at the Dade Changguo Zhou Zhi, Xue's catalog still noted manuscript copies, but the existing ones were replaced by new carved editions by Xu of Siming. Where did the manuscript copies go, and where did the carved editions come from? If not replaced, what else? Moreover, upon inspection, there was clearly a hidden cover in the floorboards, an empty space large enough for one person to go up and down. This was the fourth calamity. The decline continued until the Xianfeng and Tongzhi eras, when Xue Guan'cha engraved the catalog, but the ancient carvings that remained in the catalog were as sparse as the morning stars. It was estimated that the book catalog still had 2,056 titles, with complete notes for 1,270 titles. As for now, after several decades, the intentional and secret replacements must be ten times more than in the past. In the autumn of the Gengwu year, Mayor Yang Ziyi of the Municipal Government had the profound intention of preservation and ordered Tie Fu, Zhe Xian, Qifeng, and Yuting to investigate and prepare a catalog. Tie Fu and others, against the Fan clan's wishes, completed the task in one day. Although the time was pressing, they had a general understanding. Comparing it with the catalog written by the Fan clan in their own cleanup, it should not be too far off. The total was 936 titles, totaling 8,871 volumes, about half of Xue's catalog. Among them, there were still 250 or 60 that were intact, but most belonged to one or two volumes, about one-fifth of Xue's catalog. However, there were more than 200 titles that were not in Xue's catalog. Most of the complete ones belonged to this category. Is it because old things are easily scattered and new things are easily preserved? As the number of volumes increased, the fewer that remained. Therefore, the number of titles seems impressive, but the number of volumes is actually quite small. Among them, the most complete is the geography category, with more than 95% preserved. It is unknown whether geography is different from other books. Other books should be ancient, but geography should be modern. Ming dynasty local chronicles can be used to study the past but are insufficient for examining the present. Because they are unsuitable for the times, their completeness is fitting. In addition, no stone inscriptions or rubbings remain. More than ten pieces of stone carvings are still safe and sound. There are books that originally had dozens of volumes, but only one or two volumes remain. In addition, the Complete Illustrations and Commentary on the Book of History still has 4,074 volumes, about half of the original book. The Sancai Guangzhi, a kind of leishu (encyclopedia) similar to the Yuanjian Leihan, was annotated by Ruan with 1,184 juan and 237 volumes. By the time of Xue's catalog, 132 volumes still remained, but now only 42 volumes remain. It is likely that someone is gradually plotting to seize this book. It is heard that this time, during the arrest of thieves, someone confessed to being hired to steal this book. In the future, the situation will not reach the point of complete loss. Only then will we know that the stricter the sealing, the more covetous the crowd, and the more covetous the crowd, the faster the loss. Qin destroyed weapons to stop the chaos, but Chen She rose up and Xianyang was burned. Russia implemented autocracy to prevent change, but the revolutionary party rose up and the throne was lost. The principle is the same. The person who collects books reads them himself and has his children and grandchildren read them. Self-reading is only a few decades. Accumulating wealth for descendants and not being able to guard even this little bit, what is the point of strictly confining and deep locking? Even if the descendants want to see it, they cannot, let alone peruse it by hand and recite it. There is nothing worse than suppressing the nature of books and losing the use of books. For the Fan family, the best strategy is to allocate funds to have their ancestors reorganize the incomplete parts and supplement them completely, establish a special person to manage them, and make them available to local people, calling it the Shilang Library to popularize Shilang's virtue and perpetuate Shilang's spirit. If they estimate that they cannot achieve this, then they should transport them to the public sector and have the public bear the responsibility for reorganization and preservation. Those descendants who can read can still visit and study from time to time to share and assimilate the virtue and spirit of their ancestor. If they cannot read at the moment, they can wait until their descendants can redeem them. Public management is certainly more sustainable than private management; this is the middle strategy. First, transfer the Sancai Guangzhi, which outsiders want to steal, to lithographic printing to spread it widely, which can greatly benefit scholars and, on a smaller scale, subtly eliminate spying. This is the lower strategy. If they still insist on sealing as a policy and secrecy as a doctrine, it is either tempting bookworms or preparing rations for thieves, which is a no-strategy. If Shilang knew, he would agree with me. In the year of the Republic of China, November 6, Yang Tielu of Zhongshan wrote this preface in the Tongyin Kan Shu Room of Zhongshan Park.

Educational News Highlights

The United States Will Change Its Educational Policy

Students' Graduation Determined by Ability, Not by Academic Year or Credits: The National News Agency, Chicago, 20th – The president of the University of Chicago announced today that they intend to drastically change their educational policy. Students' graduation will not be based on academic year or credits but on individual ability. Regardless of grade level, if a student can achieve university graduation results in a large subject, they will be granted a diploma. The university's president, Hutchins, told people that most students can complete their university education in two years, and there should be many who can succeed in one year. For students who already have considerable self-study, graduation in half a semester may not be impossible. The old-style academic system is too rigid and requires a change in policy to be more flexible, he said.

The Mingzhi University Dispute Intensifies

Tokyo, 21st (telegram) – The Mingzhi University disturbance has become more complicated and is effectively a strike. Today at 1 p.m., initiated by a section of the Xiong Bian Association and the executive committee, a large student meeting was held at the Buddhist Youth Association of the Imperial University, under heavy police guard. The meeting resolved to absolutely oppose the school authorities' illegal punishments and demanded that the police authorities immediately release the detained students. Representatives were immediately sent to meet with President Yokota to hand over the resolution and to meet with Police Superintendent Kuyama to demand the immediate release of the detained students.

Jinan, 21st (telegram) – Due to financial problems, the Xiangshan Orphanage in Beiping organized a walking petition group of students to go to Beijing. Ten members, including Deng Chunxi, arrived in Jinan today to petition the Department of Education to allocate funds for the 42 students from Shandong Province attending the orphanage.

Overview of Education in Huai'an County (Continued)

(3) General Education: There is one county-run junior high school in the city, currently with five grades of students, one grade each in the first, second, and third years, divided into groups A and B, with more than 270 students. The facilities include a library and a spacious sports field. The auditorium and classrooms are newly built, and the school building is quite suitable. The attached normal school has two grades and has graduated twice. Recently, due to the prolonged vacancy of the principal's position, the county government's education bureau has sent personnel to maintain it. The new principal is in the process of being recommended. There are fourteen county-run primary schools with thirty-one grades, costing 28,700 yuan. The 18th-year graduates totaled 238 students. The county-run experimental primary school currently has ten grades, 392 students, and 20 faculty members. Principal Shao Guixiang is quite research-oriented, and his work is commendable. Various gatherings of faculty, staff, and children in the school show spirit. The county-run Guyu Primary School and Sanjiao Bridge Primary School are also well-managed.

(4) Social Education: Social education in Huai'an has made considerable progress in recent years. The county-run public education center is divided into five departments: general affairs, library, editing, promotion, and science. Each department has a director, and the attached public literacy school is quite impressive. The school offers two types of programs: general and specialized. The general program is further divided into basic and advanced levels. The specialized program is divided into three courses: crafts, home economics, and business common sense. The curriculum content caters to the needs of society and the psychology of learners. Therefore, students at all levels can advance and retreat on time, with great interest. Women's class students, from noble ladies to maids, gladly mingle. There are currently 236 female students and 96 male students in the basic level, advanced level, crafts, home economics, and business common sense classes. (Last year, eight classes graduated once, with 173 female students and 26 male students.) Classes are held from 9 a.m. to 11 a.m. and from 2 p.m. to 9 p.m. daily. Each grade has two hours of classes per day. The academic performance of the students is acceptable, which is truly a rare achievement in recent years. Director Yao Renshou is enthusiastic about research, which has led to this kind of good result. The branch centers have reading rooms and lecture rooms. The experimental public school has one principal and nine faculty members, with monthly expenses of 220 yuan. There are currently six classes with 160 students. The self-compiled literacy textbook is up to the sports field, which is divided into two departments: office and guidance. There are not many types of sports, with monthly expenses of 200 yuan. The farmers' education center is outside the north city gate, with one director and six staff members, divided into three departments: general affairs, teaching, and research, with monthly expenses of 201 yuan. There are twenty-two public schools, thirty-two public reading rooms, and a public lecture hall under construction. (Remainder omitted) (End)

Tongwen School Strike Expands

Chinese and Japanese Departments Join Strike: The Tongwen School in Shanghai's West End recently provoked a strike by Chinese students due to unreasonable oppression by the school, which has lasted for more than four days. The school authorities have not yet responded. Yesterday morning at 10 a.m., the student union convened an emergency general meeting to decide on various countermeasures, and more than ten representatives from other schools gave speeches of condolence and firm support. The atmosphere at the meeting was extremely tense. They swore that they would not resume classes until they had won. The Japanese students had previously protested the dismissal of Guo and Wang, arguing that the reasons were inadequate and the procedures were improper. There had been no adequate response to the issue of 33 yuan in county expenses being economically opaque, as well as the issues of depriving them of freedom of speech and publication and banning the Jiangnan Xuebao (Japanese newspaper). Therefore, they held a general meeting the night before and resolved to sincerely unite with the Chinese students and join the strike.

Supervisor of Students in Japan, Liu Suichang, Departs for Japan

Leaves Tomorrow on the Asama Maru: The newly appointed Supervisor of Students in Japan, Liu Suichang, returned to Shanghai from Beijing. The reporter immediately drove to his private residence on Dongpu Stone Road to inquire about the departure date and conduct the following conversation: Reporter: When will you depart? Mr. Liu: After being appointed by the Ministry of Education, I originally intended to depart as soon as possible, but because all the procedures had not yet been completed, I had to wait to receive the mandate from the National Government. Therefore, I decided to take the Asama Maru to Japan tomorrow (23rd). Reporter: There are many disputes in the student affairs in Japan, and successive supervisors have felt the difficulty. I wonder what countermeasures you have in mind in the future? Mr. Liu: I studied in Japan for eight years. After returning to China, I went to Japan several times to investigate. I know the situation there very well. Every dispute that arises cannot be blamed solely on the students' fondness for causing trouble. The other parties must also bear considerable responsibility. If we can be fair and impartial, respect the law, seek convenience for students, and take care of the face of the country, and treat each other with sincerity in everything, disputes can be reduced. I have always felt that this is the purpose of doing things, asking only for cultivation and not for harvest. Revolutionaries should especially ask only what should be done, regardless of how difficult the future is. I sincerely hope to do this in the future, even if the results are not good, I will have a clear conscience. Reporter: Are there any other personnel accompanying you on this trip? Mr. Liu: In addition to inviting Comrade Zhuang Yuling to go to serve as the director of general affairs, I plan to decide on the other personnel after arriving in Japan. If the performance of the old staff is still good, I am unwilling to make too many changes, he said.

Mr. Zhang Zuoren's Recent New Discovery

Mr. Zhang Zuoren, former professor of biology at China Public School and Great China University, is studying the inheritance of protozoa at the Tao Lai Lusso Zoological Institute JUSLILUDZOOLOGIGUEJORLRLERRROUSSEAU. The college has also prepared a laboratory for Mr. Zhang Zuoren's personal use, with extremely complete content equipment. It is said that when Mr. Zhang was cultivating a certain trichomonad PARAMAE OIUMCAUDANIUM, he suddenly discovered an extraordinary form of the trichomonad, whose form was very different from the common ones, and its method of reproduction was quite similar to budding reproduction, which was also very different from common fission reproduction. This is enough to clarify the evolution of the methods of biological reproduction and its fundamental principles. Mr. Zhang once made a report on the results of the experiment in June, which caused a deep interest in the royal zoology of Belgium and was of great interest to the experts attending the meeting.

The Situation of the Jiang-Zhe Private Middle School Soccer Tournament

The Jiang-Zhe Private Middle School Athletic Association's soccer championship tournament began on Thursday at Shanghai University. Ten teams are participating, using a single-elimination system and holding a losers' bracket to determine the runner-up. The strength of each team participating this year is considered equal, with Jinling, Shanghai University, and St. John's all having championship hopes. The first and second weeks have already concluded, with Shanghai University, Jinling, Xiuzhou, and St. John's qualifying for the semi-finals. In the losers' bracket, Soochow High School has already reached the finals. Zhijiang vs. Huilan is being replayed today. A detailed analysis is as follows:

Free Talk

A Word of Wisdom

— Lanxi

People who walk in the thorns are not often hurt by the thorns because they know what position they are in and know to be careful.

Life is blind, love is blind, and all human actions are blind. The only difference is whether their state of mind is clear.

If we admit that life is just a big dream, then what kind of dream is this that makes our hearts tremble?

You should know what to hate before you know what to love. Although love and hate are contradictory, they are quite related. The deeper the love, the shallower the hate. The deeper the hate, the shallower the love.

There is an invisible market in love. It is almost like a trade, but it cannot be heavily discounted. You should feel extremely painful when love is discounted. True love cannot be bought with money; you must exchange it for your true feelings.

In the process of life, it is like walking on a rough and uneven road. Some people carefully pass through this dangerous situation, and some people fall into the dark abyss unconsciously.

Love can make you excited when you are tired, and it can also discourage active people. Fine wine cannot intoxicate people, it only makes you feel relaxed and comfortable. But love can intoxicate your entire life.

Many young men and women have many tragedies because of misunderstandings about love. What love gives them is not pain, but a good lesson.

The love that the Creator gives us is limited. Before you get the person you truly admire and love, you must not abuse your love, because when love is used up, troubles will follow closely behind you.

A Record of Wu Changshuo's Tomb Construction in Chaoshan

— Lian Weng

Chaoshan is the main mountain of Tangqi Town in Hangzhou, with a circumference of more than 20 li. It is planted with plum blossoms and no other miscellaneous trees. Poets and literati often carry wine and chant poems here. It is said that the mountain has a Song plum tree, but its sparse shadows and subtle fragrance are naturally like a painting. It is also a new scene outside Gushan. Mr. Wu Changshuo from Anji, also known as Lang Wan, once stayed briefly in Qixi, arranging a clear tour with bamboo hats and walking sticks. His leisurely mood was exclusively arranged with the mountain spirit. Burying the poetry master among ten thousand plum blossoms may not be a bad story for future generations.

Changshuo was good at seal carving. Outside of the Eight Masters of Xiling, he could win a seat. In his later years, he was covered by calligraphy and painting, calling himself Old Can and Deaf Man. The people of Fusang especially admired him. At the age of eighty-five, he returned to the Dao Mountain. Lang Wan was responsible for the matter of building the tomb, planning to buy a piece of land in Chaoshan. However, the monks of the mountain temple regarded it as a rare commodity and thought it was impossible. Although they had repeatedly discussed it, they were unwilling to agree. Finally, they obtained more than four mu of land, preparing to build a tomb. They dug mud, lifted stones, chopped thorns, and cleared bushes. It is now in good order, but the land price is more than a thousand gold.

The name of Hejing of Fox Hill is in West Lake, and his small pavilion is still there. Mr. Changshuo lived in seclusion in Shanghai, enjoying his pen and ink. His nobility is no less than that of Hejing. Burying his bones in Chaoshan with plum blossoms to accompany his soul can truly be said to be a reflection of the past and the present.

Anecdotes from the Four University English Speech Competition

— Cheng Zhizheng

The Four University English Speech Competition is composed of four schools: Jiaotong, Jinan, Guanghua, and Fudan. It is held once a year and has never been interrupted. This year, it was held at the Wen Zhi Hall of Jiaotong University. The judges, such as Dr. Wu Jingxiong, Liu Yunfang, Li Daonan, Mrs. Huang Hanliang, and Chen Liting, are all well-known figures in society. On the afternoon of the 19th, Jiaotong University was already crowded with people and vehicles. The Wen Zhi Hall was packed with people. Here are some interesting details of the event:

About Laws and Regulations: Two rules were posted at the entrance of Wen Zhi Hall, which were quite special. One was (no entry or exit during the speech), and the other was (no applause after the speech). The former was probably to prevent disorder and prevent the speakers from concentrating, while the latter was probably to prevent emotionalism and hinder the judgment of fair people. The consideration was very thorough and could be used as a model for other speech competitions.

Talking About Love Science: The topics of the speeches by the representatives were quite interesting. The topics of the two female representatives were both on women's issues. Miss Zhu Yaozhen of Jiaotong University spoke on (Women's Sports), and Miss Chen Meier of Guanghua University spoke on (True Women), which attracted a lot of attention from the audience. The most wonderful was Mr. Peng Qixin of Fudan University, whose topic was (The Importance of Love Science). He cited ancient evidence and talked about love, saying that if love is not studied with scientific methods, it is difficult to achieve satisfactory results. For a time, the audience could not help but laugh.

Female General's Talents: The two female representatives who participated this time achieved very good results. Chen Meier of Guanghua University spoke eloquently and shocked the audience. Miss Zhu Yaozhen of Jiaotong University had a good attitude and a beautiful voice, which was rare. It is said that Miss Zhu usually practices very hard, and she often goes on stage to recite in the early morning. When Dr. Wu Jingxiong gave his personal comments, he praised her endlessly and praised her as a very promising speaker. It is said that she won first place in the individual competition at Jiaotong University's preliminary competition.

Dr. Wu's Witty Remarks: Before the awards were presented, Dr. Wu Jingxiong gave a speech. Dr. Wu said that someone had just talked about the science of love, and he should ask him for advice. He said that he himself was not good at giving speeches, but he felt that it was a pity that Chinese people spoke English, otherwise he would have spoken in Ningbo dialect today, which would have been even better. He also said that someone's voice was too low, almost like whispering in someone's ear. He was sitting in the back row and could not hear without a telephone. The audience burst into laughter.

Chen Liting Felt Ashamed: Mr. Chen Liting, the general manager of the YMCA, left after the judges finished their judging, but he did not leave the gate of Wen Zhi Hall. He was specially called back by the chairman and asked to present the awards. Chen said in his speech that the award presenter has always been a beautiful lady, and the recipient also feels supreme honor. Today, the chairman asked me to present the awards. I am not a lady and my face is also admired by you all. I feel extremely ashamed. As a result, Guanghua University won the championship and received a silver cup and a pennant.

Many Female Guests: There were many female guests in the venue that day. The fragrance of clothes and hair added a lot of color to the venue. After an investigation, it was learned that this large group of female guests were actually students from Guanghua University who came to cheer on their classmate Chen Meier. Since Guanghua won the pennant, they all smiled and returned happily.

A Record of the Chrysanthemum Gathering at Dongjiadu

— Wood and Stone Hermit

Yesterday was the date of the Chrysanthemum Gathering at the Dongjiadu Fire Administration. I was also invited. I drove there at about 6:00 PM. When I arrived, I climbed the stairs to the second floor. There were more than a hundred pots of colorful chrysanthemums, which were already a pleasure to see. The third floor was even richer. Most of the products from the San You family were luxurious and gorgeous, like the attitude of the Taiyuan son who came in a fur coat. The products from the Xiaoguan Garden were tall, elegant, and strange, which was in line with the Tao family's style. In particular, the one named "Xia Ding Shang Yi" was antique and was a rare item among the fine varieties. There were also four new varieties this year, one shaped like a bun with messy hair, like the wife of a warlord, colored light green; one colored light yellow, shaped like a hydrangea ball, but with belts and curls that do not reveal the flower heart; one colored Yang Fei, with fine tubes staggered to form a flying shape; and one colored light purple, shaped slightly the same. Solicit nominations, although many guests come to nominate, but the evaluation cannot be determined. At 7:00 PM, the guests were seated. The speakers all praised it as a spectacle. The dishes were presented one after another, and everyone drank to their heart's content. It is a pity that I could not drink much, which was a disappointment to the famous flowers. It is truly rare to have such an elegant and leisurely event in the flourishing and extravagant area of Shanghai. As for the elegance and cleanliness of the furnishings and the appropriateness of the arrangement, they are still extra things.

A Record of Dr. Tang Yaoqin's Medical Skills

— Yuyun Shanren

It is better to be a good doctor than a good prime minister. Although the two have different paths, their hearts to save the world and help the people are the same. My old friend, Dr. Tang Yaoqin, has always held this purpose. Before graduating from Zhejiang Provincial Medical School at the end of the Qing Dynasty, he witnessed the corruption of the Qing government and was worried about it. Therefore, he joined the party and traveled north and south, using medical skills to carry out his ambition. Dr. Tang was involved in the Xinhai Revolution, the Second Revolution of Gui Chou, and the Yuan-ousting campaign of Bingchen. After Yuan died and Li succeeded him, Dr. Tang devoted himself to reading, specializing in the medical classics of the Qing Dynasty. He studied the "Huangdi Neijing," "Suwen," "Zhang Zhongjing," and "Sun Simiao." He exhausted his efforts and thought with the ancients. He once said that the medical theory of our country is more subtle than that of Western medicine. Nowadays, it is gradually declining because general doctors only seek profit and do not pursue in-depth study, which makes Western medicine have a great tendency to replace it. Although Dr. Tang is a Western doctor, he cannot bear the loss of the essence of the country, and he uses scientific methods to improve and promote it. A few days ago, my wife's old illness recurred and she vomited blood. She was unable to stop the bleeding for several days, and her condition was critical. The doctors were helpless. I telegraphed from the front and rushed back, and urgently asked Dr. Tang to diagnose and treat her. He used both Chinese and Western medicine, and one medicine turned the situation around. After several visits, the blood stopped suddenly, and it was like a miracle cure. Although Dr. Tang does not boast about his medical skills, those who have broken their arms three times cannot surpass him. In recent years, he has organized an Eastern Medicine Research Society dedicated to researching Chinese medicines and chemically producing powder. He has invented a special medicine such as Xuegui, which is specially used to treat various bleeding disorders and is invariably effective like a god. Shen Jian, a medicine specially used to treat uterine diseases, such as tonifying blood, regulating menstruation, metrorrhagia, vaginal discharge, pre-pregnancy, and postpartum, is especially a gynecological medicine. There are also many effective medicines for various diseases of men, women, old and young, which cannot be described in detail. Countless relatives and friends have had intractable diseases that have been cured by Dr. Tang's diagnosis and treatment or by taking the elixir he invented. Although there are many Chinese and Western doctors in Shanghai, there are not many who are as knowledgeable in both Chinese and Western medicine as Dr. Tang. I know Dr. Tang deeply and have repeatedly persuaded him to go out into the world to achieve his original intention of saving the world and helping the people. Dr. Tang agreed to hang up a pot in the spring, so I will first introduce him in a word and tell the sick to know where to ask for help. (Dr. Tang is currently located at No. 58, Baokang Lane, Maisai Erdi Road, French Concession, along the road)

A Record of the Young Calligrapher Zhang Qi

— Rui Hongchu

Mr. Zhang Taiyan is a master of Chinese studies in the contemporary era, and his literary name fills the world. He is also good at writing seal characters. He once received a scroll of seal characters from Mr. Zhang, and the brushwork is vigorous and lovable. Yesterday, Mrs. Zhang Tang Guoli and his son Zhang Qi came to the Minghua Store. Qi is seven years old, lively and lovely, and his words are excellent. His fingers are longer than ordinary people, about four inches long, sharp, thin, and soft, shaped like ivory tablets. Mr. Zhang named him "Qi" because of this. He is also good at calligraphy. A few months ago, when Mr. Ma Xiangbo celebrated his ninetieth birthday, Qi once wrote a couplet, which was praised by everyone. I took the opportunity to ask for a couplet and was honored to have him write it in one go. Watching his calligraphy, the brushwork is like dragons and snakes, which is even more improved than in the past. He is truly a child prodigy.

Travels in Nanyang (79)

— Linghua

Arrived in Yangon on the 27th, already within the Indian border. Yangon was originally a port in Myanmar but has long been a province of British India. Though the people of Myanmar have been striving for autonomy, and it has been granted, its politics, education, and culture are entirely Indian, vastly different from East Asia. Reaching this point is like entering another world, different from the previous one. First, Myanmar is a purely Buddhist country for over a thousand years. Second, women in Myanmar hold a very high position. Third, although Myanmar is Indianized, northern Myanmar, near Yunnan's Pianma and other areas, has much contact with China. There are quite a few people from Yunnan in northern Myanmar and China, hence Buddhism is also very flourishing in Yunnan. The most famous is Chicken Foot Mountain near Yunnan. Wu Meicun's poem says (Pu'er and Cangshan are the Zou and Lu of Buddhism). From this, the Buddhist relationship between Yunnan and Myanmar is evident. Upon first staying at the Mingli Inn, I immediately visited Master Daojie of Longhua Temple, who was the master who initially ordained me. The Master has been the abbot of Fayuan Temple in Beiping for many years.

That temple was where the Qing emperors received ordination. Tagore was welcomed here the year before. The Master has traveled in Myanmar for a long time and kept diaries of his travels in the border areas of Yunnan, upper Myanmar, and central Myanmar. He has conducted in-depth investigations and research on the history of Myanmar's relationship with China and the customs of the Burmese people. He has traveled to India twice and says that Myanmar has a very rich collection of Buddhist scriptures. He was invited to translate Nepali scriptures, which are also rich. The Buddhist statues are beautiful, surpassing those everywhere, especially the statues of Ceylon, which are even more beautiful than those in Yangon.

At this time, Myanmar was already in the rainy season. It rains all day long. According to tradition, no matter who enters a temple or pagoda, they must take off their shoes. Taking off shoes is a sacred custom for the Burmese people. I mentioned before that a major incident occurred because a British official refused to take off his shoes. Master Daojie described it in detail. It happened in Mandalay, the old capital of Myanmar, where a British military officer, a brigade commander, refused to take off his shoes and clashed with monks. A monk cut his face with a knife. Seven or eight monks were arrested, leading to a major revolt by the Burmese monks and people. The matter was taken to London. The British Emperor decreed that British subjects should abide by the customs, traditions, and etiquette of each country they visit and should not refuse to take off their shoes. Thus, the Burmese won the lawsuit, and the morale of the entire Burmese people was greatly boosted. From this, we can see the British ability to pacify small countries. Their dominance over various ethnic groups is no accident. After this incident, anyone entering a temple area, even without entering the interior, must take off their shoes. It is said that only Wang Jingwei was specially permitted to not take off his shoes when he visited the Shwedagon Pagoda once. However, that incident occurred before the Burmese people's lawsuit against the British military officer was won.

European Travel Correspondence (81)

— Liu Haisu

Diary of a Tour of Italy

(III) Ten Days in Rome (IV)

The Eternal City—La ville eternelle

June 1st. Spanish Masterpieces Exhibition and Japanese Modern Painting Exhibition. 36 (Jesus Stripped of His Garments - El Espolio) This is Greco's most famous and valuable masterpiece, completed in 1579. It is a decorative painting for the Toledo Cathedral. The crowded and complex warriors exhibit an unusually solemn style. Christ and his apostles are filled with somber and bleak visages. The entire painting is a combination of simple two-color combinations of blue and yellow, blue and green, green and red, orange and blue, and blue and red.

41 (Saint Martin and the Beggar) This is a powerful and tragic contrast, a feeling of morbid excitement, expressing an extraordinary depiction of deep inner life.

Velasquez was the master who succeeded Greco and founded the Spanish school. He was skilled at portrait painting. In 1623, he went to Madrid to become a court painter. Encouraged by Rubens, he traveled to Italy twice to copy many of Titian's paintings. He completed his realism after being influenced by Titian and Ribera. His maturity was accelerated by his contact with Venetian painters, and their influence transformed his style. Soon, he succeeded in conveying natural truthfulness as a painter. Although he was a court painter of magnificent portraits, he also loved to paint cripples and the working class. This exhibition included many of his portraits and copies of Titian's paintings, which France had never seen before. The lightness, transparency of his colors, and his aerial perspective had never been achieved to such a degree before.

Goya was a great painter of the late 18th century. He maintained the Spanish tradition while being a pioneer of Impressionism. His dynamic and unrestrained brushstrokes could touch the power of life and serve as the foundation for modern art.

Morilo, a religious painter, was one of the most deeply influenced by the Florentine school. Although he was a disciple of Velasquez, their painting styles were completely different.

Editor's Note: This manuscript was received a few days ago due to late delivery and is now being published as a supplement.

The current price for Java raw sugar and December futures sugar were both 7.9375, and the price for January of next year was 8.00, showing no rise or fall compared to before. The association market scheduled a plate of Dutch sugar No. 24, coarse sand white, which was arriving in large quantities. With slow sales, the market looked even more sluggish, with offers at 7.55 taels with no buyers. No. 20 middle sand white was at 6.7 taels, finely ground sand white at 7.6 taels, No. 10 Dutch red at 6.4 taels. Both sales and purchases were quiet, and the market was generally flat and dull. Transactions in Japanese sugar were withering. Lower-grade goods also seemed to drop in price. N mark price was still 7.65 taels, YT mark 7.55 taels, YRO mark 7.075 taels, TM mark 7.1 taels, TX mark 7.725 taels, TK mark 7.55 taels, YP mark 7.875 taels, J mark 7.95 taels. The market condition was weak, and plate transactions were also quiet. Jinfahao sold 2,000 bags of current No. 20 medium sugar, with a value of 6.7 taels. The market was not surprised that the original 3,000 bags could not be sold through.

North-South Goods, Fungus Market Flat

Recently, not many fungus have arrived, but the market has sufficient inventory. However, traders' appetite is not very smooth. Both Guangdong and Fujian provinces have reduced their harvests. As for the local mainland, the transactions are scattered. Yesterday, the top-grade large fungus sold for 170 taels, the native brand fungus for 110 taels, and mixed fungus from 102-103 taels to 100 taels. The market looks flat.

Metals and Eastern Goods, New Lead Wires Arriving

After the source of new lead wires was deemed scarce, the standard prices rose sharply. No. 16 to No. 20 were estimated at 12.5 taels per load, and No. 21 to No. 25 sold for 15.5 taels, but the market had little inventory. Therefore, the general industry firms were actively purchasing Japanese goods to prepare for market sales. As a result, the port of Zhanjiang is very active now. It is estimated that the various companies have four to five thousand bundles in storage. Fortunately, customer sales are still strong, so the market prices have not fallen back. It was found that 560-70 bundles were opened yesterday, with Tianjin and Hankou traders making the most progress.
